  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();

      initializeSiwa();

  <span id="freeText1577314520187850787" style="display:none">Maximum Ride and her faithful friends stand ready to face the two greatest threats that humankind has ever known--now combining forces in an unbeatable plot to destroy life as we know it once and for all. And this time, the enemy<i> </i>truly <i>can't be stopped</i>. The danger mounts just as the boy genetically engineered to be her "perfect match", Dylan, has finally worked his way into Max's heart--and just as her beloved Fang unexpectedly returns to the flock. An explosive confrontation between the two boys with a claim to Max's heart ensues, and the entire world hangs in the balance.<br /><br /> In this powerful and moving latest sequel in James Patterson's epic fantasy series, fans will finally get the answers they've been waiting for--and an ending full of shock, surprises, and the greatest conclusion you never saw coming.</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer149911453" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer7224150695737118731">please note: this review was written when i was like 13. im so sorry. please dont judge me<br/><br/>Is it really called The End of Maximum Ride? Oh, well. Okay, I really, really, really, really, really, really, really, really, REALLY hope Dylan and Max do NOT get together. If they do, Team Fang needs to organize a group bonfire of all Maximum Ride books and get a party to go murder James Patterson. <br/><br/>WE.<br/>NEED.<br/>FAX.<br/><br/>I mean, seriously, 95% of all Maximum Ride readers are on Team Fang. What a wimpy 5% James Patte</span>
  <span id="freeText7224150695737118731" style="display:none">please note: this review was written when i was like 13. im so sorry. please dont judge me<br /><br />Is it really called The End of Maximum Ride? Oh, well. Okay, I really, really, really, really, really, really, really, really, REALLY hope Dylan and Max do NOT get together. If they do, Team Fang needs to organize a group bonfire of all Maximum Ride books and get a party to go murder James Patterson. <br /><br />WE.<br />NEED.<br />FAX.<br /><br />I mean, seriously, 95% of all Maximum Ride readers are on Team Fang. What a wimpy 5% James Patterson will be pleasing if Dylan and Max get together. Like, end of Fax, beginning of Mylan. Or Dax. Whatever. I also hope Angel is still like she was in ANGEL and not her usual traitorous backstabbing self. I also hope Nudge has more than, what, 5 lines? She barely said ANYTHING in ANGEL. Ella, Dr. Martinez, Jeb and Gunther Hagen will also probably come back and play a big role, unless they're all dead, or something. I don't even WANT to think about it.<br /><br />So, yeah. GO TEAM FANG. <br />Dylan + Max = BAD. <br />Fang + Max = GOOD. <br />Dylan + Maya = ...um...sure... <br />Iggy + Ella = Fine. Doesn't matter either way. <br /><br />PLEASE, PLEASE, PLEASE DO NOT HAVE MAX AND DYLAN GET TOGETHER. PLEASE.<br /><br />EDIT: Yesss! It's called Nevermore, not the "End of Maximum Ride"!! Now, I have no idea what Nevermore means, but it's better than "The End of Maximum Ride". So I'm happy.<br /><br />DOUBLE EDIT: Whoa, I actually really like the cover. It's pretty and mysterious at the same time. I am totally psyched for this...<br /><br /><br /><b>FINAL REVIEW:</b><br />Oh, where to begin? Right off the bat, I'd like to say that if you haven't read the book yet, do not continue with this review. I know, I know, I'm always tempted with the spoiler brackets too, but just. Don't. You will regret it.<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Now that that's over and done with, I think we should all stand back and give James Patterson a huge round of applause. He definitely ended it with a bang(literally). Way to go, James. Thanks for writing this.<br /><br />Maya. Oh, Maya, Maya, Maya. I really want to smack you, Maya. I'm not ashamed to admit, that when she died, I literally whooped. Call me heartless--I just never liked her character. And the fact that Fang was getting all. . .romantic with her, disturbed me on so many levels. Um, helloooo, Mr. Fang, you're currently flirting with the clone of your ex-girlfriend. Ladies, if you ever meet a guy that does that--trust me, he's not over you. Anyways, it was an interesting death scene, but I'll get to the whole Ari thing later.<br /><br />Admittedly, I was not expecting Star and Kate to betray Fang. That really surprised me. It was a cool plot twist though, and it gave them a little more depth than they had before. Ratchet and Holden were still. . .hrm, well, not as interesting. <br /><br />Now we get back to Ari. I actually kind of liked that plot element, mainly because it put Jeb in a position that made him look like he actually cared about Ari, which I liked. Makes Jeb a little harder to hate, which he needs, in my humble opinion.<br /><br />I was really surprised that Gunther-Hagen made NO reappearance whatsoever!! Really startled. He was mentioned at one point to Dylan, I believe, but still. <br /><br />Moving onto. . .Mark, and the 99 percenters. Oh, and the ending! Joy. Hm. Weeeeell, to put it bluntly, it seemed anti-climactic. There was a huge build-up to this virus, and then a meteor explodes. Having chatted with a friend of mine, I know I'm not the only one who went ". . .wait, what?" at that part (more about the ending later). The 99 percenters seemed to be almost unnecessary--they were basically the Doomsday Group people all over again. <br /><br />The Flock. Their roles in this novel really ticked me off. Nudge--her sole purpose in this book was to whine about school, go on a date, then whine about school. This make Ruthie unhappy. Dx Iggy &amp; Gazzy--they both had really small roles. Nothing super important, which, once again, makes me rather unhappy. I wish they played bigger parts. Total--back again, but not much to do, same old, same old.<br />And then there's Angel. I'm not sure if I'm happy or displeased with the fact that she's Max's voice. It was a very interesting plot element, but does that mean she was the voice for all the other members of the Flock? What about her own voice? And how was Jeb able to control some things in Max's voice if it was Angel the whole time? It didn't fit 100% with the rest of the story, but I'm willing to let that slide, because at least it was explained. :P I really hated her scenes in the school, mostly because I don't like it when she suffers. Except when she's a traitor/backstabber, which she wasn't.<br /><br />Prepare for ranting--now I talk about <i>him</i>. Dylan--beautiful; perfect; funny; popular; Max's other half; and for part of the book, a rampaging idiot who tries to kill Fang!! Oh, the joy of hormones. I'll talk about Fang more in the below paragraph, but basically, I'm a fan of him. I'm not a fan of people who punch him in the face. Although, it's about time. That fight has been coming for a while now. I'm not sure I followed why Dylan decided to go rampaging and play whack-a-car, because to me, personally, I don't think that idea was the most intelligent one on Dyl's part. Oh well. He was DEFINITELY more developed in this book than the others, and I will say, I liked him more in this book then I have in the past two. He had more depth, and I didn't want to throw the book against the wall every time he spoke, which is a plus.<br />The Fangalator. I was impressed with him in this book--not as sulky as he has been in the past. And, way to go Fang for manning up and going back to Max! Go him. Yay. He seemed a little more mature here then has has been--I think this book was a big step for a lot of characters--and I was really happy to have him back with Max. I don't have a lot to say about him, really, but I was pleased overall with his role.<br /><br />There were some characters brought back in this book that have previously had a bigger role then they did in this one; mainly Dr. Martinez and Ella. Dr. Martinez was mind-controlled by Jeb for part of the book and she was working at the school on Angel. Other than that, and a few spots at the end, she didn't do much. Sadly.<br />Ella was there, and she was a-okay. No mention of her getting wings or anything. Hrm. She DID kiss Iggy though, and that was fantastic!!<br /><br />The whole paradise thing was pretty cool. There were a few chapters in that area where I was deliriously happy--Faxness and Paradise, what more could a reader want? Clearly, more. I should've smacked myself upside the head for thinking that it would be a happy ending. As I said earlier, I found the ending to be anti-climactic. I was a little let down that there was no virus and a meteor just exploded above the earth, raining down chaos and fire and blahblahblah. Ahem. Pardon me for not finding that as cool as it would be if all their skin rotted off their bodies. Especially Dylan! That would be cool. One thing, though--at the end there, it gave NO confirmation to whether Iggy, Gazzy, Nudge and Ella survived. We knew that Dylan, Fang, Max and Angel survived, but it didn't confirm to whether the rest of the flock lived. O_O I really hope they lived, I really, really hope they lived.<br />Once again, I roll my eyes at the concept that there are tons of other mutant kids--but now living on an island with the richest guy in the world! Okay, I'll shut up now.<br /><br />Finally, before I bring this review to an end, I must talk about Max. Max, what shall we do with you? For quite a while in the middle of the book, I was prepared to grab my pen and replace Max's name with Bella Swan. Goodness gracious, Maximum, could you quit your whining? It was the helpless maiden all over again. HOWEVER, it wasn't as prominent as the last book, and I was thrilled with that. She definitely pulled it together and had limited boy-sob-fests. Which was good. Very much so. <br />She ended up realizing she loved Fang (;D), and realized that Dylan was not her man. I loved, loved, LOVED that. As you all know, I'm a Fax supporter. ^-^ Really, though, she could've stopped going on about Dylan's gorgeous looks and just pulled it together sooner. Ah well, she's not perfect. Far from it.<br />I was positive she was going to die in this book--and she did, sort of. Not completely. I thought she was dead for about 3 minutes there, but I was too shell-shocked to actually do anything about it. Fortunately, Max was not dead, just...floating! Or something. In shock, probably.<br /><br />I may have missed some things I wanted to talk about, seeing as it's pretty early in the morning as I'm writing this, so if I did, I'll come back and edit later. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><br />On a whole, I would give this 2.5 stars. I liked some parts, and disliked others. It wasn't my favorite book, but I didn't hate it as much as, say, Final Warning.<br />I'm going to go back and re-read it again in the next couple days, when I'm not so excited and reading really fast in case there are any bits I missed. I do tend to do that.<br /><br />Thanks for reading my review. I'd love to know if you guys agree with me, or what your opinions are!<br /><br /><br />~Ruthie~<br /><br />PS: Now that I have the book in my possession, I really do think Max looks like an old lady on the cover. She's got. . .white hair. . .</span>
  <a data-text-id="7224150695737118731" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_195122677" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/195122677" />
    <a title="Rachel" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5972322-rachel"><img alt="Rachel" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1389071189p2/5972322.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/195122677?book_show_action=true">Aug 05, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel" href="/user/show/5972322-rachel">Rachel</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer195122677" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6371430144979178138"><b>EDIT: I finished! Below is my review of pretty much the rest of the series. Writing a review on just this book would be too hard.</b><br/><br/>Before I even begin, let me begin by apologizing for what I'm sure will turn into a rant. I'm sorry.<br/><br/>First off. Nevermore. What the heck was James Patterson thinking? The first three titles ("The Angel Experiment," "School's Out -- Forever," and "Saving the World and Other Extreme Sports") were great. They were definitely, definitely unique. I could even live with "The </span>
  <span id="freeText6371430144979178138" style="display:none"><b>EDIT: I finished! Below is my review of pretty much the rest of the series. Writing a review on just this book would be too hard.</b><br /><br />Before I even begin, let me begin by apologizing for what I'm sure will turn into a rant. I'm sorry.<br /><br />First off. Nevermore. What the heck was James Patterson thinking? The first three titles ("The Angel Experiment," "School's Out -- Forever," and "Saving the World and Other Extreme Sports") were great. They were definitely, definitely unique. I could even live with "The Final Warning" (although, let's face it, it was anything but final). But once he started naming his books by the names of the main characters, the titles just lacked excitement and general appeal. A book called MAX wouldn't attract my attention if I just happened to run into it at the bookstore. <br /><br />Secondly. Oh jeez. I know this is what most people are saying/thinking about this book, but I'll say and think it anyway: Fang had BETTER get his sorry butt back to Max and ditch Maya. Maybe even kick Dylan's butt. Maybe even throw Maya and Dylan IN a ditch. I would go so far as to say it was poor - no, absolutely absurd - planning on JP's part to spend the first, what, six? books building up this close-to-perfect, adorable, and maybe even funny relationship between Max and Fang. To bring Dylan into this series and virtually cut Fang out of the picture was cruel and foolish. It was just stupid, that's what it was.<br /><br />Thirdly. Where, where, WHERE did the real flock go? I miss the old flock. Angel was cute, she was nice, and she adored/looked up to Max. Gazzy was also cute, he was funny, and he actually blew things up once in a while. Nudge talked a lot, she supported Max, and she was INVOLVED in the story. Iggy, heck, he blew things up left and right, he annoyed Max, and he messed around with everyone. Fang, well, he was Fang. He was untouchable, strong, serious, and yet passionate about the flock. Max. She was a freaking awesome, back-sassing, butt-kicking, sarcastic leader. In Angel, she was too busy whining to Dylan about Fang and being a lump of mush who needed to GET HERSELF TOGETHER. She didn't even beat anyone up in Angel, did she? That's just not the Maximum we know and love. And Total barely said a word in Angel. James, sir, you need to take a gander at your first few Maximum Ride books and fix what you've destroyed. Because it's gotten out of hand.<br /><br />Fourth. The plots have grown increasingly less believable and bearable. I mean, at first it was being chased around by mutants, narrowly escaping death's grip, taunting the Erasers, and mouthing off to Jeb. And now? It's speeches on global warming and organizations that somehow plan to take over the world's human population through its minds. What happened?<br /><br />Fifth. Dylan is, what? Eight months old? Maybe nine or ten months by now, I'm not sure. Max is fifteen YEARS old. That is a difference of approximately 170 months (around 14 years, give or take a few months). I do believe it would make more sense for a fifteen year old girl to date/fall in love with a fifteen year old (hint, hint: Fang) boy. Dylan should not love Max. Maya would be a more suitable girlfriend for him, since she is closer in age, and Fang isn't in love with her. At least, I don't think Fang is in love with Maya.<br /><br />Sixth. I'll shut up now. I can't tell you how many long hours I've spent both ranting and drooling over this series (after reading book 4 and beyond, most of my time has been spent ranting, rather than drooling). Sorry for rambling. Now, if you'll excuse me, I have to go re-read the original three books in order to regain my sanity. Thanks for reading.</span>

  <span id="freeText15224211759049126002" style="display:none">Bah-humbug!<br><br>Where to start, where to start? Who CARES about Fang's regrets?! Who CARES about Dylan's love issues?! Who CARES if Max can't pick between the two guys!<br><br>Because, dear readers, there are more than TWO GUYS ON THE WHOLE FREAKING PLANET!! When will the heroine just wake up and see "Hang on a sec. These guys are both stupid and I should find someone else!" <br><br>So the plot was all kind of:<br><br> - Max's POV: Whine about Fang and make Bambi eyes at Dylan<br> - Fang's POV: Feel all tingly when talking to Maya, but feel guilty about it 'cause of Max<br> - Dylan's POV: Max Max Max Max Max Max Max Max Max...<br> - Angel's POV: AHHHHHHHH!!! Someone HELP ME! Ooh, I can see the present as well as the future!! AHHHHHHHHHHH!!<br> - HALT. Actual plot occurs. There is a 99% plan going on. Evil scientist stuff...AGAIN.<br> - Max's Pov: (see previous)<br> - Fang's POV: Maya dead so now speaks 'gruffly' and makes 'intense gaze' stuff at Max<br> - Dylan's POV: (see previous) + Shit I hate Fang why can't he go die in a hole?!<br> - Angel's POV: AHHHHHHHHHHHHHHH!!<br> - Mention plot briefly<br> - Max's POV: (see both previous mentions)<br> - Fang's POV: ...<br> - Dylan's POV: ...<br> - Angel's POV: AHHHHHHH- oh, forget it!<br><br>And so on.<br><br>And at ANY POINT did it mention that Max had grey hair?<br><br>NO.<br><br>NADA.<br><br>Also...what is Nevermore? The book didn't even MENTION the WORD!!<br><br>ME NO COMPREHENDE!!!<br><br>This book had pained me. Greatly. I will now have to find a GOOD book and recover from this harrowing experience!<br><br><br>______<br>Pre-reading Review:<br><br><a href="http://s1080.photobucket.com/albums/j333/countess4/?action=view&amp;current=tumblr_lyzosjP6CK1qltuygo1_250.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380374639ra/728823.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>My reaction exactly!!<br><br>I can't stand how this series is now about three things:<br><br>1.) Max and her issues<br><a href="http://s1080.photobucket.com/albums/j333/countess4/?action=view&amp;current=tumblr_lzclaoChXw1qb5gkjo1_500.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380374639i/728824.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>2.) Fang and his whole "I think we're better apart things<br>3.) Dylan and his puppy dog tailing of Max<br><br>In other words it has turned into a cross between Bold and the Beautiful and Twilight. <br><br>And the fact this series has been dragged out over 8 books? What is this?!! The series would have gotten 5 stars had it ended in Max (Book 5). Fang + Max, the flock is happy, the world is saved. But no. Just keep on adding books!! I totally scan-read the last one. And that cliffhanger? It wasn't even a cliffhanger! To me it was more like "Oh, we need an excuse for another book so here is a totally boring cliffhanger. Angel is captured. Again. The world needs saving. Again." END THE SERIES. Please. For good this time!!<br><br>Don't get me wrong. I loved the first lot of books. I was obsessed! But now, I think the series needs, needs, NEEDS to be drawn to a close and to concentrate on the REAL plot - like the first couple of books did. They were about SAVING THE WORLD. NOT, about WHICH GUY DO I CHOOSE.<br><br>Please Nevermore. I don't care if Max is 80, with grey hair (cover?!) and Fang decides to relocate to Mexico. Just END THE SERIES WELL. Save the world and let us go back to our lives!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="15224211759049126002" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/161699623" />
    <a title="Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4506078-kyle"><img alt="Kyle" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/m_50x66-82093808bca726cb3249a493fbd3bd0f.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/161699623?book_show_action=true">Apr 17, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kyle" href="/user/show/4506078-kyle">Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">People who don't care if it makes no sense</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4506078-kyle?shelf=give-me-a-break">give-me-a-break</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4506078-kyle?shelf=what-the-everliving-fuck-was-this-s">what-the-everliving-fuck-was-this-s</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4506078-kyle?shelf=awesome-cover">awesome-cover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4506078-kyle?shelf=2012">2012</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4506078-kyle?shelf=overhyped">overhyped</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4506078-kyle?shelf=sequel-not-as-good">sequel-not-as-good</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4506078-kyle?shelf=post-apocalyptic">post-apocalyptic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4506078-kyle?shelf=lust-not-love">lust-not-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4506078-kyle?shelf=massive-dissapointment">massive-dissapointment</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer161699623" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10386594472437671147">Okay, here we fucking go. If you think that this book and this series and James Patterson/whatever ghost writer he hired this time is the best thing since sliced bread, and think this review is "wrong" or "too harsh" or "it was just a book!" than don't even bother commenting. If you say, "Oh well I'm afraid I'll have to disagree on such and such" that's fine. Do not tell me my review was wrong or question why I felt this way about something. If I got something wrong, you can point that out, it's</span>
  <span id="freeText10386594472437671147" style="display:none">Okay, here we fucking go. If you think that this book and this series and James Patterson/whatever ghost writer he hired this time is the best thing since sliced bread, and think this review is "wrong" or "too harsh" or "it was just a book!" than don't even bother commenting. If you say, "Oh well I'm afraid I'll have to disagree on such and such" that's fine. Do not tell me my review was wrong or question why I felt this way about something. If I got something wrong, you can point that out, it's fine. However if my facts are correct, do not tell me I'm wrong.<br><br>Oh yeah, and there will be <b> a lot of spoilers </b>. You were warned.<br><br>Alright, now we begin. Well, I guess I should say, where exactly do we begin? Back in November of 2010 I picked up the first installment in this series because I was looking for something cool and fun. A lot of my friends were going crazy over this series since the sixth installment had recently come out. So, I go to Barnes &amp; Noble, and get the first one. I loved it, and devoured the other five that same month. I noticed that they weren't as good around the fourth book. I thought the third was the best, than the first, then the second, and then I read the fourth and I wanted to throw up from the sheer stupidity of it. I mean, you go from bird kids flying around stopping bad guys to going to Antarctica stopping global warming?<br><br>Excuse, but what the fuck was that shit? That continues into book five, and then is suddenly dropped out of nowhere. Now, listen: if you're going to ramble about global fucking warming for two books, you can't fucking drop it and move on to the next topic! CONSISTENCY is key here! <br><br>The sixth was a huge 300 paged melodramatic piece of crap about how "Fang would be the first to die" or whatever. Then the seventh was a completely different thing about some stupid apocalypse where the humans would die and mutants would live. Um, okay. What the fuck was this apocalypse suppose to be? Why didn't the idiotic humans realize that the 99% of people who would die were going to be them? And no, do not pull the "brain washing" card on me. Just no.<br><br>Now, let's get onto this piece of shit. So, first off, what was the plot you might be wondering? Well, I cannot figure out what the fuck was the point of this? Do you know why the GR synopsis is six sentences? Because nothing fucking happens. THERE WASN'T A FUCKING POINT TO THE LAST FUCKING BOOK IN THIS FUCKING SERIES. Let's see what did happen though:<br><br>1. Max and the flock begin going to high school because poor little Dylan wanted to.<br><br>2. Dylan is instantly uber-popular and everybody loves him<br><br>3. Nudge gets some random boyfriend and hates her wings<br><br>4. Angel's dissappearance is finally aknowledged <br><br>Now, wait a minute. We're going to fucking talk about #4 for a moment longer. Gazzy, who is Angel's older brother, does not give a fucking shit that his little sister is "dead"? Did he? Well, I wouldn't know since Mr. Patterson's ghost writer must have forgotten they were siblings that were protective of one another. <br><br>5. Fang's flock is attacked by Ari, who guess what? HAS COME BACK TO LIFE FOR THE THIRD FUCKING TIME. <br><br>6. It turns out Fang has to die AGAIN. His blood has the key for fucking immortality. <br><br>7. Maya is killed in a "dramatic" showdown against Ari, and it turns out that Star and Kate backstabbed Fang.<br><br>8. Fang ditches the other two guys in his group and goes to find Max because "The Voice" is telling everybody to protect her<br><br>9. Dylan is told he must make babies with Max again and make her fall in love with him.<br><br>10. Dylan and Max have a disastrous date.<br><br>11. Fang comes back, and Dylan goes on a fucking psychotic ramapage destroying a nearby town.<br><br>12. They go and save Angel.<br><br>13. Ari and the Erasers show up once again to kill Fang, and Jeb is randomly there AGAIN, and they loose and Dr. Martinez shows up AGAIN saying she has a safe haven for them on some random fucking island with other mutants where they'll be safe from an airborne virus that the 99% Percent released to the rest of the population.<br><br>14. They arrive at the island without Dylan, who left<br><br>15. They're relaxing, Max and Fang get back together, and Dylan comes out of fucking nowhere saying something is happening in the sky.<br><br>16. Angel begs Max not to return to die with the humans, and reveals she is the Voice (oh, I will be returning to this plot hole).<br><br>17. I am not kidding you when I say this: THE SKY FUCKING EXPLODES.<br><br>18. A MASSIVE TSUANMI WAVE SHOWS UP OUT OF NOWHERE, AND MAX AND FANG PROCLAIM THEIR UNDYING LOVE FOR ONE ANOTHER AND ARE SWALLOWED BY THE WAVE<br><br>19. The first epilogue is Max's "dying words" saying it's okay blah blah blah<br><br>20. The SECOND EPILOGUE reveals that *gasp* Max survived!!!!`1``1213 Remember?! She has fucking gills! Of course she would fucking survive. <br><br>21. Her, Fang, Dylan, and Angel are looking at the island after the disaster <br><br>22. The End<br><br>Now, before we move on to review this fuckery, let us bring back up Point #16. How the fuck can Angel be everybody's Voice when she has a Voice too?! What the everloving fuck is that?! CONSISTENCY, THY NAME IS NOT JAMES PATTERSON/HIS GHOSTWRITERS. <br><br>Now, let's talk characters, the love triangle, etc.<br><br>Max has officially become TSTL. When she knows that the world is going to fucking tear itself apart, she is making a Pro-Con list about Fang and Dylan to decide which boyfriend she wants. <br><br>O.O<br><br>THE WORLD IS GOING TO FUCKING TEAR ITSELF APART. GET YOUR PRIORITIES STRAIGHT. <br><br>You know, this love triangle is simply because Mr. Patterson thinks that love triangles are "hip" and "now" so he thinks it'll help his books sell better by putting a super hot, super perfect love interest in to create romantic tension. <br><br>Fang and Dylan? What are they? Just pawns put in for the love triangle, nothing more. <br><br>The rest of the Flock is nothing after Book Three. They say perhaps a line every 200 pages, and that's all they can get. I can't even review them.<br><br>Nobody else is given any closure. Is Jeb good or bad? Where the fuck is Dr. Gunther-Haagen, who is, surprise surprise, alive? Will Ari come back to life yet again? <br><br>Writing is atrocious and inconsistent. The plot makes absolutely no sense and is inconsistent.<br><br>This whole fucking book is inconsistent.<br><br>Um, you just said 20 pages ago that the apocalypse would be the virus that the 99% group released. WHY IS THE SKY EXPLODING AND GIGANTIC TSUANMI WAVES APPEARING?! THAT IS NOT WHAT YOU JUST TOLD ME. <br><br>We're never told what happens to Nudge, Gazzy, Iggy and Total after they mysteriously run off with all the other mutants. Do they live or die? Well, that's of no concern to Mr. Patterson. As long as he got some random ending, it was fine by him. <br><br>Such a fun series - WASTED.<br><br>Absolutely <i> wasted </i>. <br><br>This is what I was feeling the whole time I was reading this piece of shit:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380348520ra/702760.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380348520ra/702761.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380348520ra/702762.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380348520ra/702763.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i> Fail Mr. Patterson. Fail. </i></span>
  <a data-text-id="10386594472437671147" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/162716965?book_show_action=true">Apr 21, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annabelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annabelle" href="/user/show/1235083-annabelle">Annabelle</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1235083-annabelle?shelf=i-own">i-own</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer162716965" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16779782616943449815">***FINAL RATING: 3.35 STARS***<br/><br/><b>
  <u>CATCHALL</u>
</b><br/>Was this book perfect? Not by a long shot. But did I absolutely love it? Yes. It had a ton of problems—don't get me wrong—but my overall satisfaction with the book was high. I do wish that some parts had been done differently, and that some of the problems had come to better solutions. But despite this book's problems, yes, I did love it. It was a fun and quick read in between some of the heavier stuff I've shouldered lately.<br/><br/><b>
  <u>THE HEROINE</u>
</b><br/><u> MAX</u><br/>So, Max. T</span>
  <span id="freeText16779782616943449815" style="display:none">***FINAL RATING: 3.35 STARS***<br /><br /><b>
  <u>CATCHALL</u>
</b><br />Was this book perfect? Not by a long shot. But did I absolutely love it? Yes. It had a ton of problems—don't get me wrong—but my overall satisfaction with the book was high. I do wish that some parts had been done differently, and that some of the problems had come to better solutions. But despite this book's problems, yes, I did love it. It was a fun and quick read in between some of the heavier stuff I've shouldered lately.<br /><br /><b>
  <u>THE HEROINE</u>
</b><br /><u> MAX</u><br />So, Max. The first time I read about Max. She was awesome. The freaking epitome of badassery. And as the series progressed—she didn't necessarily get that much worse, but there was some sort of decay. In this book I felt like she was a bit on the whiny side and didn't really focus on the big picture, but more on the little things. Even so, I don't think I could ever hate Max. By the very end of this book anyway, she seems to grow into herself.<br /><br /><b>
  <u>THE LOVE INTERESTS</u>
</b><br /><u>FANG</u><br />I love Fang. I always have. Because he's so strong, and yet also vulnerable. And I think that's the way a lot of people are, to be honest. And even though he's more of the strong and silent type, he also isn't afraid to express his feelings when he needs to. He can be incredibly, extremely sweet, and I love that. Furthermore, even if his head isn't always in the right place his heart is. Fang is easily my favorite character in these books. Easily.<br /><u>DYLAN</u><br />I don't like Dylan. To begin with, he's very—bipolar. Extremely so. He'll seem to be sweet one moment but rampaging angrily the next. No one who isn't bipolar does that. I basically can't stand him and am glad I don't have to breathe the same air as him. I dislike him that much, yes.<br /><br /><b>
  <u>THE OTHER IMPORTANT PERSON</u>
</b><br /><i>Directly translatable to "I was too lazy to think of a good header"</i><br /><u>ANGEL</u><br />Angel is definitely an important character. She's the one who can see the future, and that becomes important in the way this story unfolds. However, something really weird is revealed about her that doesn't make any sense and it just—no. I didn't like it at all—it seemed like a weak attempt to close a plot hole while it actually just created more. So, nice going.<br /><br /><b>
  <u>THE PLOT</u>
</b><br /><i>Le plot.</i><br /><br />Okay, so I'm not sure where to start. To begin with, I guess, there is an insane number of plot holes. EVERYWHERE. That was probably the most annoying thing about this book and the series in general. I was constantly irritated because things were just left hanging, not tying themselves up. I'm not necessarily a fan of super-clean endings, but messy ones are even worse. Ick.<br /><br />Now that we've gotten my whining aside…<br /><br />Essentially, the plot in this book isn't much different from the plot of the entirety of the series. Sure, there are subplots galore. But they're not the focus, and more often than not they end up just kind of fizzling out to nothing.<br /><br />One thing I will say about these books—a positive thing—is that they're incredibly quick reads and very, very fast-paced. It's easy to sit down with this book, finish it in that one sitting, and then looking up amazed at how much time has gone by. I love when a book is like that—when I can be drawn completely into its world.<br /><br />Moving on from that, though, another thing I want to say is that I did genuinely and completely enjoy reading this book. The plot was fun, and kept me interested. There was a sense of urgency to it that made it even more fun, and a suspenseful quality that hadn't really been there before.<br /><br />I loved it!<br /><br /><b>
  <u>THE ROMANCE</u>
</b><br />I really hated the love triangle that developed in these past few books, and I'm glad that it came to a solution before the book had ended and that that aspect was not left open to interpretation in a bad way. And honestly, somehow it was done well. It actually made actual sense. I'm sounding repetitive, but after the plot holes and whatnot it was really something different to see the execution here.<br /><br /><b>
  <u>THE WRITING</u>
</b><br />Ah. Yes. The writing. It's not horrid. It's unique. Max has a very distinctive and unique voice that is easy to pick up on. That part is really cool, actually. The weird part is when she says all these things that seem thrown in and random. I actually prefer James' third person writing. I'm not really sure why—I just know that I do. For some reason, it was much more enjoyable.<br /><br /><b>
  <u>THE ENDING</u>
</b><br />So, the ending. It really left a lot of plot holes open, which I am just not cool with. It was intensely frustrating and annoying at once. Even so, there was a romantic quality to it that I liked and it was sweet. It was also surprisingly happy, and although there's a lot we don't know and a lot of loose strings hanging everywhere, overall I felt pretty satisfied with it.<br /><br /><b>
  <u>WRAPUP</u>
</b><br />So yes, I loved this book! Though honestly, I'm not sure how I feel about recommending the series, since it has some serious problems that are un-over-look-able. And I just—can't. I probably won't be reading James' other books either, including his newest YA series, just because I feel like they get dragged out for an unnecessary amount of time. Still, never say never. It could happen.<br /><br />FINE.<br /><br />Find more of my reviews on <a href="http://sparkles-and-lightning.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Sparkles and Lightning</a>!<br /><br />--<br /><br />WTF?!? 20-freaking-12?!? Are you freaking kidding me?!?<br /><br />And February?!? Really?!? It's not enough to make me wait until next year, I have to wait a whole extra freaking month?!?<br /><br />(And...the date of release got moved to August. Sigh ): )<br /><br />Okay, that aside, Fang and Max must get back together. They belong together. Period. Elsewise I will be mad and probably never read a James Patterson book again.<br /><br />I love Fang. :) He's so strong but so sweet and also just so damn hot.<br /><br />Hello, I just love the cover :)<br /><br />FANG + MAX FOREVER &lt;33</span>
  <a data-text-id="16779782616943449815" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emma" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emma" href="/user/show/6219602-emma">Emma</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer205689537" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16311190148897831699"> I need to rant. No, not about Max and Dylan being together. Not about the title, not about the changes and how "sucky" the last books have gotten. I am ranting about you dumb trolls! I know I'm going to get so much hell for this, but I think you guys that are reviewing this series are ALL wrong. I made an account on this website just so I could say this, that's how mad I am. First off, why are you all saying Max should be with Fang? Why?! I loved the "Fax" couple up to the end of Fang when Fang</span>
  <span id="freeText16311190148897831699" style="display:none"> I need to rant. No, not about Max and Dylan being together. Not about the title, not about the changes and how "sucky" the last books have gotten. I am ranting about you dumb trolls! I know I'm going to get so much hell for this, but I think you guys that are reviewing this series are ALL wrong. I made an account on this website just so I could say this, that's how mad I am. First off, why are you all saying Max should be with Fang? Why?! I loved the "Fax" couple up to the end of Fang when Fang left the flock. Why? Because Fang's sorry little emo butt doesn't deserve Max. Let's recap what Fang has done to hurt the flock; left them . . . twice. Then, right after he left, he automatically went to his little blog and replaced Max with get this, Max II. Let's stop here; if a boy I loved had replaced me right after he left with my clone, I could never, ever forget. Forgive MAYBE, but forget I would never, which is why Max should NEVER get back together with Fang. EVER. Now let's move to the subject of Dylan. I hated his guts. HatED being the key word. Dylan may have entered the flock quite . . . unexpectidly but he was made to love Max. Think about it from Dylan's point of view; the person you were literally made for hated your guts and loved another person who broke it off with your love, emotionally scarred her, yet she STILL loves him and is after him (kinda). Wow. POOR DYLAN! And another thing, it wasn't Angel's fault exactly she turned on Max. Yes, I hated her in Fang, but she is only six! SIX! Muntant bird kids make mistakes too :( and in Angel, she was like Max's fricking awesome sidekick! And remember, her voice made her split up the flock. NOT. HER. FAULT! She was just following in Max's footsteps by listening to her voice. Now I know that you trolls are going to say that Fang made a mistake like Angel did and he should just pull an Angel move or something. No. Fang is fourteen. He's smarter than a six year old. Duh! Anyway, so based on my rants, here is how I think Nevermore should play out: "Maya" gets killed in some freak accident (*cough cough* MAX) and Fang's little friends freak out and say it's "too risky" and that they're out. Fang runs back to the flock. They let him back in and Dylan cusses under his breathe. Fang tries to rebuild his relationship with Max , but she pushes him away farther. Dylan then pulls Max away to talk and they make out (&lt;3) Fang sees this and freaks out. Max sees him and flies after him and they have a HUGE arguement. Max then remembers she is meant to save the world and breaks off her relationship with both Fang and Dylan. Max then saves the world with epic explosions and battles, finds Angel and Dylan becomes Max's boyfriend. The end. Further reasoning/rants: Okay so now we know my Nevermore fantasy. Like it Fax's? LOL anyway, I don't like Maya. She's annoying and I don't know why . . . oh I know: irony! Fang hated Ari for trying to kill the flock and blah blah blah but then he welcomes Maya into his flock when she did the same thing! HA! Fang is just an a**hole. So anyway, I am done. I love Maximum Ride all the way BECAUSE it makes you feel empathy, rage, sadness, etc. You guys need to know that that is what makes a book good, not the romance. Please, learn that. Okay I'm done. &lt;3 <br />***Sorry for being so obnoxious LOL***</span>
  <a data-text-id="16311190148897831699" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_370317561" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/370317561" />
    <a title="Avani" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11018895-avani"><img alt="Avani" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591751600p2/11018895.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/370317561?book_show_action=true">Jul 16, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Avani" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Avani" href="/user/show/11018895-avani">Avani</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11018895-avani?shelf=love-triangle">love-triangle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11018895-avani?shelf=letdowns">letdowns</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer370317561" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2988745260840181498">I just finished this <b>two-stars</b>-worthy book.<br/><br/>When I found out that this book, that I’ve had on hold at the library for months and months, was available for me to pick up the very day it came out, I rejoiced.<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380377435ra/732722.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Nevermore: The Final Maximum Ride Adventure. The book to end all books. Literally-- the end of the world is upon the flock.<br/><br/>I didn't <i>hate</i> this book. I’d take points off for the ending, and more for just an <i>aura</i>, of an all-action, a let’s-just-kill-someone-off-and-do-this-here-and-that-there-beca</span>
  <span id="freeText2988745260840181498" style="display:none">I just finished this <b>two-stars</b>-worthy book.<br><br>When I found out that this book, that I’ve had on hold at the library for months and months, was available for me to pick up the very day it came out, I rejoiced.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380377435ra/732722.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Nevermore: The Final Maximum Ride Adventure. The book to end all books. Literally-- the end of the world is upon the flock.<br><br>I didn't <i>hate</i> this book. I’d take points off for the ending, and more for just an <i>aura</i>, of an all-action, a let’s-just-kill-someone-off-and-do-this-here-and-that-there-because-it’ll-help-the-plot-later-on kind of attitude. I will explain this later.<br><br>We start out with the cover. Okay, fine. I opened the cover and read the inside cover flap: "One last incredible, explosive adventure with an astonishing ending that no one could have seen coming."<br><br>This is the warning that should have been projected at this point.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380384275i/742746.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The prologue. Oh, the prologue. I just absolutely <i>knew</i> (okay, I didn't really know) that Max was going to die. I had to emotionally prepare myself now, just in case my premonition would come true later on. But I won't spoil it for you, so don't worry, you can keep reading this.<br><br>We all know Max was warming up to Dylan. I had refused to accept it in the previous book, Angel, and this was me when someone said something supportive in regard to "Team Dax".<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380384275i/742747.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I was totally Team Fax. Until, well, this book. Because (the following isn't really a spoiler, but I'll spoiler alert it in case you're touchy) <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[We all knew Fang was going to come back, but I'll hide it under the spoiler anyway. Fang came back and starts being a real jerk to Dylan. C’mon Fang, Dylan has Max’s best interests in mind, dude. And then he swoops in and takes Max. Which isn’t really completely his fault, because Max is perfectly fine with being swooped up. Anyway. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> That, and Dylan has been there for Max this whole time, whereas Fang was just, well, not.<br><br>Aside from the Dylan vs. Fang love triangle drama, we have some of the usual end-of-the-world theories, with a new apocalypse-crazed group of people—actually, they’re not really new. They were born from the ashes of the old ones.<br><br>Overall, my criticism of Nevermore comes from two things. One, the aforementioned let’s-just-kill-someone-off-and-do-this-here-and-that-there-because-it’ll-help-the-plot-later-on attitude. This rests in one of many examples: Max’s decision regarding Dylan and Fang. I think I saw this decision coming, but the way the choice happened was completely whirlwind and out of the blue. I can’t say I disapprove, because, well, it’s who she loved in the end, but it was too fast for me to process. I felt like some things were done just to be done, and there was no point building tension. It’s something you can only understand when you have read the book. Another example: a character died (I won’t say who), and there’s a moment of grieving, but it all feels too convenient, as if the purpose of the death was to fill in a hole that contributes to the outcome of the plot, and the battle was just there as a reason to kill off that character. This is probably ultimately the reason for a lot of character deaths in many books, but this felt too much like it, because even I, a reader, could see it.<br><br>My second criticism was regarding the ending. This was typical Maximum Ride-quality book. All witty sarcasm, humor, and getting-to-the-point kind of writing. Just another doomsday plot… until the end. This ending was supposed to rock my socks. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380384275i/742748.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Instead, I had a generic, oh-that’s-cool-I-didn’t-see-that-coming-at-all thing after finishing. (I feel the need to point out that the previous statement was sarcastic). When James Patterson just dumps it all out on us and then runs away. I take one star off for the anticlimactic ending, the kind of ending that makes you go—<i>wait, what?</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/412125.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>…and start frantically flipping the pages, thinking, <i>no, there must be more, there must be a major cliffhanger, a plot twist, <b>something</b></i>. At least explain yourself! We don't know what happened to half the characters!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/329814.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This left the reader thinking, I guess… but this just felt like it was thought up of as a neat and tidy, convenient way to tie up the complex series that is Maximum Ride.<br><br>Well, that’s it. My overall opinion of this book can be summed up in a picture.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380384275i/742749.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="2988745260840181498" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5616015842390225952">Alright look, Mr. James i-don't-know-what-your-middle-name-is Patterson, you gotta lot to cover in this last book if you wanna make everyone happy. And I mean a LOT.<br/><br/>Let me give you a recap on your "homework":<br/><br/>1. Please, please, PLEASE tell me what the hell Dr. Chu and Brigid are supposed to be involved with. You've made them useless little dolls that aren't irrelevant to the current story at all - come on, you REALLY thought I wanted to see them again? Pul-ease. <br/><br/>2. FAX. Must I explain myself one </span>
  <span id="freeText5616015842390225952" style="display:none">Alright look, Mr. James i-don't-know-what-your-middle-name-is Patterson, you gotta lot to cover in this last book if you wanna make everyone happy. And I mean a LOT.<br /><br />Let me give you a recap on your "homework":<br /><br />1. Please, please, PLEASE tell me what the hell Dr. Chu and Brigid are supposed to be involved with. You've made them useless little dolls that aren't irrelevant to the current story at all - come on, you REALLY thought I wanted to see them again? Pul-ease. <br /><br />2. FAX. Must I explain myself one more time through your thick head? No Mr. Patterson, it is NOT a machine you use to copy something to send it to another person, that's a COPIER!! And no, it is also not a document sent over a telephone line!!!! PLEASE get them back together or else your fan base will drop and your Daniel X and Witch &amp; Wizard books will become obsolete, amazing as they both were. If you're thinking you can make an "interesting" twist by making Max and Dylan...what's the word for it...BREED, then you're out of your mind. Should you choose to fail or worse - ignore this assignment, no teen will ever read your books again, and believe me, it's sad that Daniel X and Witch and Wizard are going to go to waste.<br /><br />Side note: Patterson, I'd like you to meet <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2876763.Becca_Fitzpatrick" title="Becca Fitzpatrick" rel="nofollow noopener">Becca Fitzpatrick</a>, who has a shorter series, Hush, Hush, but has just the amount of crap as your last 4 books.<br />Now, back the the rest of the assignment:<br /><br />3. Make Angel the way she was before. No, not from book 5, keep going...yes, all the way from book 1, when she was adored by Max and not turned into a serial fortune teller. Your work has almost been finished since book 7, but alas, 'tis not done yet. <br /><br />4. Make Gazzy, Iggy, and Nudge and even Total TALK for once. You made them useless little dolls that just utter words here and there while Max, Fang, and *bleah* Dylan the stars of the show! Even <strong>Fang's Gang</strong> talks more than them - and they just appeared! Everyone LOVES Iggy, and Nudge, and Total, and even Gazzy, so make them have a say in all this! What do they think of this situation? And isn't there ANYONE ELSE besides herself Max can talk to?<br /><br />5. Speaking of Max, I'd like you to meet Nora Grey, from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2876763.Becca_Fitzpatrick" title="Becca Fitzpatrick" rel="nofollow noopener">Becca Fitzpatrick</a>'s <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6339664.Hush_Hush_Hush_Hush_1_" title="Hush, Hush (Hush, Hush, #1) by Becca Fitzpatrick" rel="nofollow noopener">Hush, Hush</a> series. She reminds me of you Max, because she just keeps whining and whining about something, and when she finally gets what she wants, she throws it away! Max and Fang right now are exactly like Nora and Patch at the start of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7791997.Crescendo_Hush_Hush_2_" title="Crescendo (Hush, Hush, #2) by Becca Fitzpatrick" rel="nofollow noopener">Crescendo</a> (book 2), except in the end Max ends up with DYLAN.... (FAX!!!!!!!!)<br /><br />I think that's all the "homework" you need, and think wisely about doing it, because if not your fan base will drop like flies.</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/166766071?book_show_action=true">May 09, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Freefallen ~ YA Reviewer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Freefallen ~ YA Reviewer" href="/user/show/5096004-freefallen-ya-reviewer">Freefallen ~ YA Reviewer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer166766071" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2554009969884286598">WOW.<br/>YOU.<br/>DID.<br/>NOT.<br/>SEE.<br/>THAT.<br/>ONE.<br/>COMING.<br/>AT ALL.<br/><br/>I have mixed feelings about this book. Whilst I'm happy at the way it ended, I still felt that James Patterson had a lot of things built up throughout the series which he then proceeded to place giant roadblocks in front of.<br/><br/>For example. This isn't really much of a spoiler, so I'm not going to enclose it. The book ANGEL (previous installment) is nothing more than a filler. Okay, maybe there's some information you need to know. Here:<br/><br/> <b>"There's a crazy bunc</b></span>
  <span id="freeText2554009969884286598" style="display:none">WOW.<br />YOU.<br />DID.<br />NOT.<br />SEE.<br />THAT.<br />ONE.<br />COMING.<br />AT ALL.<br /><br />I have mixed feelings about this book. Whilst I'm happy at the way it ended, I still felt that James Patterson had a lot of things built up throughout the series which he then proceeded to place giant roadblocks in front of.<br /><br />For example. This isn't really much of a spoiler, so I'm not going to enclose it. The book ANGEL (previous installment) is nothing more than a filler. Okay, maybe there's some information you need to know. Here:<br /><br /> <b>"There's a crazy bunch of people trying to take over the world called the One Light. The leader's called Mark. Some are hybrids and can therefore hypnotise people. They kidnap Angel and experiment on her. They blow up Paris. Fang makes his own gang. Max falls for Dylan. Iggy and Ella fall in love."</b><br />That is <i>pretty</i> much all you need to know. You're welcome, I saved your behind from 300 angst-filled pages.<br /><br />Speaking of Ella, the last time we saw her in ANGEL... didn't she run away? To... somewhere... to get wings? Or something like that? In THIS episode, she bounds out of nowhere all happy and smily - without wings - like nothing happened... Or did I miss something in that installment... Please correct me if so.<br /><br />AH-nother thing. From Book One, <i>"The Voice"</i> is telling Max to save the world. WELL. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Max doesn't really save the world... She just survives the apocalypse. Along with other mutants. AND- <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[-the apocalypse we speak of... We don't actually know much about. There was about a page on how most of the world caught this big disease, and at the same time the sky tears open and the earth gets shaken up a bit. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I'M SORRY. We waited 8 books for this very moment, and all that happens is whipped up in a couple of pages?<br /><br />Meeeeh?!<br /><br />On the other hand, I do actually love this book.<br /><br />Why? SPOILERS.<br /><br /><b>THINGS I LOVE:</b><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Max and Fang get back together. That's right. The impossible happens.<br /><br />Max and DYLAN start to get on better.<br /><br />Dylan completely loses his marbles and goes destructo.<br /><br />Iggy and Ella are officially shipped.<br /><br />Angel lives. And is actually the Voice. Creepy girl.<br /><br />The Flock goes back to being the way it was. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>THINGS I DON'T LIKE:</b><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Fang's Gang gets disbanded. RATCHEEEEEEEET! 8'(<br /><br />Star and Kate are baddies.<br /><br />Maya dies.<br /><br />Everything that ever happened in ANGEL is suddenly irrelevant.<br /><br />The ending we'd been waiting for 8 books later wasn't all it was cracked up to be. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />However, I gotta hand it to JP - you didn't do half bad writing these books. He deserves a round of applause! Clap clap clap.<br /><br />And hey, even if you didn't like the ending - there's always FanFiction, right? ;)<br /><br /><br /><br /><b>Previous-Rant-Before-I-Read-It.</b><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Maybe this isn't the last book.<br />Comeon, book 4 was entitled "The FINAL Warning", then the books after that launched into "Maximum Ride: The Protectors" series.<br />I think we're gonna have to face it guys.<br />FAXNESS IS OVER.<br />But the preview indicates that Maya might have died...<br />I think Mr. Patterson is planning on this series having an interesting twist at the end, but...<br />Maybe Dylan, Maya etc. are all part of a dream? Like in STWAOES?<br />Why hope.<br />My depression has gotten worse.<br />IF NONE OF YOU LIKE THE ENDING TO THE BOOK, FILM YOUR REACTIONS THEN SEND CLIPS TO ME! It'll be a great Youtube vid!!! ;D My email is dragonsinger[at]live[dot]co[dot]uk<br />This book needs to come out NOW. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

<div id="review_306652993" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/306652993" />
    <a title="Filippa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8594680-filippa"><img alt="Filippa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1342476908p2/8594680.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/306652993?book_show_action=true">Apr 04, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Filippa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Filippa" href="/user/show/8594680-filippa">Filippa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9781846057779" href="/book/show/15810735-nevermore">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8594680-filippa?shelf=end-of-series">end-of-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8594680-filippa?shelf=books-i-own">books-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8594680-filippa?shelf=summer-reads-2012">summer-reads-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8594680-filippa?shelf=taking-too-long-to-come-out-sequels">taking-too-long-to-come-out-sequels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8594680-filippa?shelf=ending-that-did-the-series-justice">ending-that-did-the-series-justice</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer306652993" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6358511206444199061">EDIT EDIT EDIT. REVIEW REVIEW REVIEW. SCROLL DOWN PAST ALL THIS OLD STUFF TO READ IT. SPOILER FREE.<br/><br/><br/>Oh, Max, Max, Max.<br/>Where did it all go wrong? (well...we KNOW where it went wrong, but let's just keep with the rhetorical).<br/>After so many years of reading these books, investing my time, heart and soul into them, its all come down to this.<br/><br/>Every Maximum Ride fan will tell you straight that this series has plummeted downhill faster than Max on overdrive since The Final Warning - it's just an accepted </span>
  <span id="freeText6358511206444199061" style="display:none">EDIT EDIT EDIT. REVIEW REVIEW REVIEW. SCROLL DOWN PAST ALL THIS OLD STUFF TO READ IT. SPOILER FREE.<br /><br /><br />Oh, Max, Max, Max.<br />Where did it all go wrong? (well...we KNOW where it went wrong, but let's just keep with the rhetorical).<br />After so many years of reading these books, investing my time, heart and soul into them, its all come down to this.<br /><br />Every Maximum Ride fan will tell you straight that this series has plummeted downhill faster than Max on overdrive since The Final Warning - it's just an accepted fact. And yet still we've stuck with it, hoping and praying something can be salvaged from the train crash that Patterson has made of. <br /><br />First, let me get one thing absolutely straight; I adore these characters. Utterly, truly love them. With one notable exception, to whom I will get to later. <br /><br />What I hate is what James Patterson has done to them, and to the MR series as a whole. The first three books were fantastic. I fell in love with Max's personality, and plunged face first into her world. Gripping, thrilling, God-damned hilarious - just brilliant.<br />Then we get book 4. We all know what an abomination that was. <br /><br />It picked up at book 5 - our Max was BACK. Less of the lecture, more kick-butt action MR does best. (Alongside some Faxness ;) ) We forgave JP his FW failings, and took it as a momentary blip that was in the past.<br /><br />And then book 6. Oh, book 6. Where to begin?<br />Well, put it this way, I read it in Waterstones on the day of its release, desperate to find out what happened. And somehow the book ended up being thrown to the other side of the room, whilst angry sales assistants glared at me. <br /><br />What happened to our beloved characters? Where was Nudge/Gazzy/Iggy's roles in the story? Since when did Fang and Max turn into gloop?<br />JP completely tore away their personalities, and threw them into situations which just wouldn't have happened. It was a betrayal, not only to the readers, but to Max.<br /><br />Book 7 was worse, if that is indeed possible. Just an appalling plotless drivel that again took all characters OOC. <br /><br />And now, fellow reviews, there is only Nevermore that can sort out this stupid mess, and bring back our Max. And sadly, I dont see it happening. I think the main problem is that James Patterson never planned that the fans wouldnt like the whole Fang/Dylan/Max saga. Oh, it worked for Twilight and The Hunger Games. What he didnt realise is that it would just fall flat in MR.<br /><br />Because, blatantly, we HATE Dylan. I'm pretty sure I can say that on behalf of 99.9% of the fanbase. We don't like him, don't see the point in him and sure as hell don't want Max with him. <br />Max and Fang were just an unquestioned constant in the novels. We didnt WANT a triangle - there was absolutely no need. And its just ruined the whole thing.<br /><br />The worst part about it is that its looking increasingly likely she'll end up with Dylan. <br />In her recent 'blogs' its clear JP is trying to persuade the readers to take to him. The readers are simply not.<br />Take this recent 'blog update' by Max:<br /><br />"I've told you what I've been obsessed with lately. And you've made it clear what you've been obsessed with: why does everyone want to MURDER Dylan?"<br /><br />^See? <br /><br />Besides the whole Dylan thing, there are far too many loose ends that need to be tied up properly in this book. I don't trust JP to at all make a success of them. <br />Nevermore - like it's title - is looking more and more like a complete disappointment, ending the series on a complete low.<br /><br />And I ache for it, I truly do, because I love the characters, and their world so much. They've been done a complete injustice by their author, which is surely the biggest sin a writer can committ. <br /><br /><br /><br />UPDATE: I've just been reading the preview chapters and I want to HURL. Its the biggest load of rubbish I've ever read. I want to grab each character and shake them until they either die *cough* MayaDylan *cough* or get back to the characters they were.<br /><br />One chapter its all Max going gooey eyed over Dylan, but oh, isn't she supposed to love Fang? But oh, Dylan smells so good and his eyes are blue like the sea and blah blah blah. <br /><br />And the next its all Fang going gooey eyed over Maya, but oh, she's not Max even though she looks like her. But oh, being with her is so magical and blah blah blah.<br /><br /><br />EVERY. SINGLE. CHAPTER.<br /><br />Where's my kick butt Max and Fang? Believe me, I have hormones too. But funily enough they dont make me turn into a pathetic mush. It's sickening, really.<br /><br />Oh, how I hate you James Patterson. <br /><br /><br /><br /><br />EDIT EDIT EDIT!!!!!!<br /><br />Okay, guys. Nevermore was released on August 2nd in the UK. It's now 2am the next day and I've just finished reading it.<br /><br />To be honest, the only coherent thought I have about it is: DA FUQ WAS THAT?<br /><br />I swear, the whole thing was a bit of a blur. <br /><br />I suppose the main thing is: was it good?<br />Well, maybe. Like I said, I don't really know what to think of it at the minute. And I was so ready to hate it. But to say I liked it is maybe stretching it a bit. I think I was content with it.<br /><br />This was the end. Every ounce of love, hate and frustration we fans have been building up for years was riding on this book. This was the make or break of how the series will be remembered.<br /><br />Personally, it could have been a lot worse. It really could. <br /><br />The first half, though, I was all ready to throw into a bonfire adorned with a James Patterson Guy on top whilst I danced around the edge waving 'The Angel Experiment' in the air. It was exactly the drivel we've been putting up with ever since Dylan entered the scene. (Oh Dylan. How I hate you)<br /><br />However, it began to change half-way through. It's like it was almost back to the Maximum Ride of old. The characters were almost IN character (you tried, Patterson). But like I say; almost.<br /><br />I much preffered the Max of this book to the Max of, say, everything after book 5. She still had her OOC moments, of course, but every now and then there were glimpses of the kick butt girl we know and love. <br />She reminded me why I ever loved the series in the first place. <br /><br />I'm not going to comment on the whole Max/Fang/Dylan fiasco, because I don't want to ruin it. I won't even give away whether I'm crying with joy or am currently hunting JP down as we speak. If you really cant wait to find out what happens though, drop me a message and I'll let you know.<br /><br />Ah, the ending. I guess this is what the whole thing was about, right? The official Facebook page made such a hoopla about it being the END of MAXIMUM RIDE. She was going to DIE, DEAD, FOREVER. <br /><br />Did she? Well....spoilers ;)<br /><br />No seriously though, that ending was weird. So rushed, unexplained, oddly set out. At times I was staring at the page thinking WHAT THE HELL IS GOING ON HERE PEOPLE?<br /><br />Did the end justify the story? Jury's out on this one I'm afraid. <br /><br />Did the end justify the means? With Maximum Ride, always.<br /><br />Now, I'm going to post those ten questions we were promised would be answered in Nevermore. I won't give away those answers, but I will post my own reactions alongside.<br /><br />1.Who will Max finally choose--her beloved Fang or steadfast Dylan?<br /> No comment.<br /><br />2.Who is The Voice Max hears in her head?<br /> I admit, I was surprised. And completely unconvinced. <br /><br />3.Which Member of Fang's Gang will betray him?<br /> Ah, Fang's Gang. How I hated you all. All I'll say here is: memberS<br /><br />4.Whose side is Angel really on?<br /> Will we EVER know who's side she's on? Okay, maybe I'm being a little unfair here, because Angel goes through hell in this book.<br /><br />5.Is Jeb trying to protect Max and the Flock? OR is he working for the bad guys?<br /> As with Angel, I don't think we'll ever really know. <br /><br />6.Will Iggy ever regain his sight?<br /> What a strange question. <br /><br />7.Why did the Flock evolve to be able to breathe underwater?<br /> Clever. Quite clever. It makes sense now.<br /><br />8.Will Iggy and Ella ever be together?<br /> Like I'm gonna spoil the fun for all you Eggy lovers out there :)<br /><br />9.Is the apocalypse the result of human folly and hatred, a disease, a natural disaster, or an invasion from outer space?<br /> I have NO idea. Like I said, the ending was a bit of a haze. Personally, I think it was aliens. Just 'cause.<br /><br />10.Can Max really save the world?<br /> Could YOU save the whole world?<br /><br />11.And the most important question of all: who will die? (You didn't think it would end with out someone dying, did you?)<br /> Oh happy days, oh happy DAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAYS<br /><br /><br />And make of that what you will.<br />I'll probably write a proper review once everyone's had the chance to read the book. <br /><br /> <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6358511206444199061" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
